                        adRefreshRateDeskSectionBucket = parseInt( strikeConfigDynamicProps.adRefreshRateDeskSectionBucket, 10) || 30,
                        adSizesDeskSectionBucket = strikeConfigDynamicProps.adSizesDeskSectionBucket || [],
                        adPrefetchMarginDeskSectionBucket = parseInt( strikeConfigDynamicProps.adPrefetchMarginDeskSectionBucket, 10) || 500;

                    window.foxstrike.cmd.push(function(Strike){
                        Strike.loadAd({
                            target: '#desktop_desk-hp-lb3',
                            iu: 'desk/hp/lb3',
                            sizes: (function(){
                                var adSizesDeskSectionBucket = strikeConfigDynamicProps.adSizesDeskSectionBucket || [],
                                    adSizes = adSizesDeskSectionBucket;
                                return (adSizes && adSizes.length > 0) ? (adSizes.split(',')) : [];
                            })(),
                            pos: 'desktop',
                            props: {
                                adRefreshRate: adRefreshRateDeskSectionBucket,
                                adPrefetchMargin: adPrefetchMarginDeskSectionBucket
                            }
                        });
